< Review>
Currently in the Navy/Submarine Service stationed in Groton, CT. The racks on board are horrible, back is wrecked...yada yada yada. Anyways. got the chance to take some leave and come home. This place just opened up, being always in search of something new, I checked it out.

As soon as you walk in you're greeted by the very friendly receptionist. Ask what you're looking for in a massage, have you fill out a questionnaire to better understand your needs.

After you're done with the check-in you're guided to the spacious tranquility room. This place smells NEW! Theres cucumber water standing by also.

Now for the massage, best massage you will ever have! Jessica is incredible. She takes the time to get to know where your problem areas are, and works wonders on all your knots. Very professional. You won't be disappointed!<//Review>

Highlights:
Competitive and reasonable priced
Great showroom
Coordinated steps, including very detailed plans
Expert designer, Matthew
Experienced and knowledgeable Project Manager, Jeff
Fantastic Cabinets (Starmark) and quartz counter tops (ADP Granite and Marble, Inc.)
Stayed on schedule
Immediately notified us of any issues
Fantastic results and better than expected.
Suggestions:
Know your style. Use pictures from PInterest and hard copies, this gives designers an overview of your style.
Spend some detailed time in Remodel Works show room.
Go over your final plans in great detail, this is your most important step. Remodel Works will not start until you approve every detail. Changes in the middle of a project can be costly and impact your plans. The plans cover electric, paint, plumbing, counter tops, cabinets, tile, doors, appliance set-up areas, faucets, lighting. Don‚Äôt count on things you said verbally, check to see if your requests are in the plans as many things are going on during remodel planning. Other than small changes we stayed with our plans.
You pick your own major appliances and flooring which gives you price options, medium or higher end.
From beginning to end (seven weeks, which was exactly the Remodel Works estimate) they stayed on schedule. There are very busy days and some down days.
My remodel was extensive and included a large kitchen, family room with fireplace, bathroom, laundry room and office. Two designers Matthew and Eric arrived at my home and did a great assessment of the job. This was my fourth company who had all done in-house assessments. It was my family‚Äôs first large remodel. I was impressed with the designer‚Äôs experience and their pricing was one of the best of the four companies. We continued to work with Matthew on our ideas that I had collected pictures over several years. Matthew added many suggestions, including some cost savings with the fireplace that turned out fantastic. Matthew greatly enhanced my style and taste.  We then met with the project manager Jeff. He spent a great deal of time going through the project in immense detail. He made some very practical suggestions which enhanced the remodel foot print.
Highly recommend Remodel Works!< /Text>

< Review>
I really wanted to try this place since I saw their great deals for sake. Inside is really cute and clean. It is a bit small, but not crowded. We were seated immediately.

We ordered the short ribs, okonomiyaki fries, two beef bibimbap, and the chicken jjim. Of all the dishes, the chicken jjim was our favorite. The chicken and noodles were super tasty. The sauce went well with the bibimbap. I loved the fries and would highly recommend those for an appetizer. The short ribs were a great deal too. I think one downside was that there were no sides/banchan, but that's okay!

I loved this place and definitely plan to visit again soon. They have a great happy hour discount on sake. Their menu is pretty extensive and have a great selection of small plates. They're also doing take out for quarantine!</Review>

It's been awhile since I gave a 5 star review but this little hidden gem sure deserved it. I saw this fairly new place a week ago while running errands and stopped by for lunch with a friend today.

Seafood Jeon $6.50
Korean savory pancake with mixed seafood
5* This was one of the best dishes, 2 small pancakes perfectly cooked. Crispy and tender at the same time.

Boneless Fried Chicken (spicy or soy garlic) $7.50
Bite size Korean style crispy boneless chicken with your choice of flavor
5* Another hit, chicken was cooked to perfection and the sauce was perfectly seasoned.

Popcorn Salmon $6
Bite size fried salmon with spicy
4* The salmon was just slightly overcooked for my liking but still divine.

Corn Cheese $6
Corn with creamy sauce and cheese on sizzling pan
3* This was average, nothing spectacular. Next time we will order the slicked beef salad instead.

I forgot to take a picture of the dessert, the Mango Panna Cotta was definetly a nice touch to end a delicious meal. I gave this restaurant 5 stars because the waitstaff was excellent. Great service with a smile!< /Text>

<UserId.>106396898732398420545<//UserId.><username>Carlos Hernandez< /username><time>1551909655958</time><rating>2< /rating><Review>Stopped in after seeing a recommendation from a friend and plenty of good reviews on here. I wanted to try the katsu-don but when I asked the waitress about it she said they could not make it that evening...so I decided to order the bulgogi bowl and some okonomiyaki fries.

I didn't expect the okonomiyaki fries ($6) to be good but actually they were excellent. The fries had a McDonald's like texture but gourmet with kewpie mayo and katsu sauce finished with bonito flakes on top. Excellent.

Then the bulgogi bowl ($12.95) appeared. This bowl was a sad bulgogi bowl with disappointing small slices of meat that tasted like every Korean AYCE BBQ place I've ever been to. There was tons of green salad (with no dressing) and rice that filled the whole bowl probably at least 80% of the bowl with some clear noodles.

I would much rather pay more and have good bulgogi than pay less and have a disappointing experience. The bulgogi marinade was also super sweet, acid reflux inducing...overall just not good. I would not order it again.

The ambiance is nice here and its a good place to go with friends and maybe order some tapas, but if you really love Korean food you might find yourself disappointed at Jijime.<//Review>< pictures>
None</pictures>

<user>111237305138351139264</user>< username>
Annmarie Cerveny< /username>
<date>1527621057188<//date><Rate>1< /Rate>< review>
I live in Patterson, I took my father-in-law to dinner to try out this restaurant for the 1st time.  We sat outside along with a couple of other customers and we made our order and also notice that the other customers around us were having issues with their order. When the food arrived it was only my father-in-law's food and as he politely waited for my food to arrive I told him to eat his food. When my tri-tip sandwich arrived, I noticed 4 thin slices of meat on the sandwich and the rest was lettuce, along with cold fries. I told the waitress and she took it to fix it. By the time it was returned to me my father in law finished his dinner and my sandwich had a few more pieces of meat on it. Plus it did not feel like it was fresh, more like placed in the microwave. As I got a box, my father in law paid the bill. I couldn't let him pay for the worst tri-tip sandwich I've ever had. So I asked for a refund for my meal that I did not eat. They did offer me another sandwich, but I declined their offer since they already had the chance to fix it.
I gave this place a 2nd & 3rd try after that experience, and still was not impressed with their overpriced food, which was not that great. I will not go back there again.
I would rather go to Apricot's BBQ in Patterson and pay a little more.< /review>

< Review>
My car began making knocking sounds whenever I drove so I decided call them to take a look since I've used their services before for engine & coolant change as well as a transmission drain and fill and was satisfied with their prices and service. Decided to come back for a repair.

Called them in the morning around 9:30am and let them know I wanted to have it looked at but didn't have a ride back and they said to bring it in and they could drop me off. I lived nearby.

Arrived and was checked in and greeted by Renton.  Friendly guy. Looking around, the lounge area was clean, and they had Keurig coffee ready for brew, a water dispenser, a little candy tray, as well as a large bin of what looked like circus animal crackers.  I thought it was a bit weird to have all the snacks and coffee next to the entrance of the bathroom but the bathroom looked very clean for an autoshop.

After checking in, Renton told me their person who drops people off was off doing just that and wasn't available but would be able to have me dropped off in my own car by another associate if I was ok with it. Which I was.

I later received a call and was told of the issue (breaking or broken engine and transmission mounts) and of the estimate to repair. Parts and labor included (they would have to order the parts) and they would have it done by the end of the day. Googled around and it seemed like a fair price so I said yes.

What I was bothered by if anything at all with this experience was that I had to call them at the end of the day to ask for the status of my car since it was closing time for them and they hadn't called me yet. My assumption is that they were very busy. The person I was able to speak with said the parts came in late and they would be finished by the next day late morning.  It was more like near end of day but I wasn't in a rush to get it so long as it was before end of day.

Received my car and it was sounding better than before without the knocking and other sounds of course.  I'm satisfied with my services and the price at which they charge and will be taking my cars back for other services including maintenance services.</Review>
